      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses in the 15th century
       </b>
       . During the period 1401 to 1500 there were 222
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 77 were partial, 65 were annular (three
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 61 were total (one non-central), and 19 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 6 different years: 1414, 1432, 1443, 1461, 1479, and 1497.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Dates are given using the
       <a href="/wiki/Julian_calendar" title="Julian calendar">
        Julian calendar
       </a>
       .
      </p>
